				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Concerto for 2 Violins in D minor, BWV 1043 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>

<table>

</th>
<td>3 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1718–20?
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
